  <script>
   (function () {
      if ("PerformanceTiming" && "PerformanceObserver" in window) {
          const observer = new PerformanceObserver(function(list) {
              for (const entry of list.getEntries()) {
                  const metricName = entry.name;
                  const time = Math.round(entry.startTime + entry.duration);
                  if (typeof newrelic !== 'undefined') {
                      newrelic.setCustomAttribute(metricName, time);
                  }
              }
          });
          if ("PerformancePaintTiming" in window){observer.observe({entryTypes: ['paint', 'mark', 'measure']});}
          else {observer.observe({entryTypes: ['mark', 'measure']});}
      }
      
      // from https://github.dowjones.net/wsjdn-tesla/dj.svc.end_user_monitor/blob/master/lib/page_perf_monitor.js#L161-L195
      if (window.PerformanceObserver) {
        // Holds current CLS score, as changes over time.
        var _cumulativeLayoutShiftScore = 0;
        // Perf Obserever tracks CLS
        var clsObserver = new PerformanceObserver(function(list) {
          var entries = list.getEntries();
          for (var i=0; i<entries.length;i++) {
            // Only count layout shifts without recent user input.
            if (!entries[i].hadRecentInput) {
              _cumulativeLayoutShiftScore += entries[i].value;
            }
          }
        });
        clsObserver.observe({type: 'layout-shift', buffered: true});
        // Sends the final score to newrelic once when tab change/link change occurs.
        document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', function() {
        if (document.visibilityState === 'hidden') {
          // Force any pending records to be dispatched.
          clsObserver.takeRecords();
          clsObserver.disconnect();
          // Log the final score to the console.
            if (typeof newrelic !== 'undefined') {
              newrelic.setCustomAttribute('layout-shift', _cumulativeLayoutShiftScore);
            }
          // console.log('CLS:', _cumulativeLayoutShiftScore);
        }
        });
      }
    })();

           fuboTV reports first $100 million quarter
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p class="article__summary">
          Shares of fuboTV Inc. undefined were down 3% in extended trading Tuesday after the live-sports streaming service reported spikes in quarterly revenue and subscribers. The company said fourth-quarter revenue nearly doubled, to $105.1 million, from a year ago as its number of subscribers improved 73% to 548,000. In a letter to shareholders, fuboTV said it expects sales of $101 million to $103 million in its current quarter, and subscribers of 520,000 to 530,000. FuboTV's stock is up an astounding 373% over the last 12 months. The broader S&amp;P 500 index undefined is up 29% over the past year.

        <div class="article__content">
         <h3 class="article__headline">
          <a class="link" href="https://www.marketwatch.com/story/nordstrom-tops-quarterly-views-promises-better-inventory-management-2021-03-02?mod=home-page">
           Nordstrom tops quarterly views, promises better inventory management
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p class="article__summary">
          Shares of Nordstrom Inc. undefined fell more than 1% in the extended session Tuesday after the retailer beat analyst expectations for its fourth-quarter profit and sales but detailed inventory snags. Nordstrom said it earned $33 million, or 21 cents a share, in the quarter, compared with $193 million, or $1.23 a share, in the year-ago period. Revenue fell to $3.65 billion from $4.54 billion a year ago. Analysts polled by FactSet expected Nordstrom to earn 16 cents a share on sales of $3.58 billion. Heading into the holidays, Nordstrom experienced delays in inventory flow, which led to higher inventory levels at the end of the year, it said. "Heading into 2021, we're taking steps to improve our inventory position," Chief Executive Erik Nordstrom said in a statement. For the first quarter, Nordstrom guided for revenue to grow more than 25%, with online sales representing about 50% of sales. Shares of Nordstrom ended the regular trading day down 1%.
         </p>

         <div class="article__content">
          <h3 class="article__headline">

        <div class="element element--article no-image " data-docid="1369780757" data-guid="dec4d8ab-2608-41ad-b2c4-f75b55aadd83" data-msgid="61609" data-timestamp="1614721107000">
         <div class="article__content">
          <h3 class="article__headline">
           <a class="link" href="https://www.marketwatch.com/story/api-reports-a-weekly-climb-of-more-than-7-million-barrels-in-us-crude-supplies-sources-say-2021-03-02?mod=home-page">
            API reports a weekly climb of more than 7 million barrels in U.S. crude supplies, sources say
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p class="article__summary">
           The American Petroleum Institute reported late Tuesday that U.S. crude supplies rose by nearly 7.4 million barrels for the week ended Feb. 26, according to sources. The data also reportedly showed gasoline stockpiles fell by 9.9 million barrels, while distillate inventories also declined by about 9.1 million barrels. Crude stocks at the Cushing, Okla., storage hub, meanwhile, edged up by 732,000 barrels for the week, sources said. Inventory data from the Energy Information Administration will be released Wednesday. On average, the EIA is expected to show crude inventories up by 1.3 million barrels, according to a survey of analysts conducted by S&amp;P Global Platts. The survey also shows expectations for inventory declines of 2.9 million barrels for gasoline and 3.9 million barrels for distillates. April West Texas Intermediate crude  was at $59.57 barrel in electronic trading, compared with Tuesdays settlement at $59.75 on the New York Mercantile Exchange.
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
